Source Code

These source code files are a reconstruction of Sundance, the Apollo 9 LM (Lunar Module) AGC (Apollo Guidance Computer) flight software, created from binary dumps of original core rope program modules, as follows:
  • B1 — Revision 292
  • B2 — Revision 302
  • B3 — Revision 302
  • B4 — Revision 302
  • B5 — Revision 292
  • B6 — Revision 306
This means that source code does not represent a specific historical revision of Sundance, but rather a mixture of the three released versions. Nonetheless, it is capable of flying the whole Apollo 9 mission. This source code matches the binary dumps, as closely as feasible, but 100% match is not possible, due mostly to changes in memory addresses at which code and variables were allocated in different revisions of Sundance. Refer to this list of explanations for each binary mismatch.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Sundance are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

019633,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
019634,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
019635,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of a reconstructed, mixed version of Sundance
019636,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the Lunar
019637,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 9.
019638,000007:                                                                                                  ##              No original listings of this program are available;
019639,000008:                                                                                                  ##              instead, this file was created via disassembly of dumps
019640,000009:                                                                                                  ##              of various revisions of Sundance core rope modules.
019641,000010:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
019642,000011:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
019643,000012:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
019644,000013:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-06-17 MAS  Created from Luminary 69.
019645,000014: 
019646,000015:                                                                                                  ## Sundance 302
019647,000016: 
019648,000017:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
019649,000018:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
019650,000019:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
019651,000020:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
019652,000021:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
019653,000022: 
019654,000023:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
019655,000024:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
019656,000025:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
019657,000026:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
019658,000027:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
019659,000028: 
019660,000029:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
019661,000030:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
019662,000031:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
019663,000032:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
019664,000033:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
019665,000034:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
019666,000035:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
019667,000036:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
019668,000037:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
019669,000038:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
019670,000039:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
019671,000040:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
019672,000041:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
019673,000042:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
019674,000043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
019675,000044:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
019676,000045:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
019677,000046:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
019678,000047:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
019679,000048:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
019680,000049:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
019681,000050:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
019682,000051:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
019683,000052:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
019684,000053: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
019685,000054: 
019686,000055: 33,2000                                           BANK     33                                    
019687,000056: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
019688,000057: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
019689,000058: 
019690,000059: 24,2000  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
019691,000060: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

019973,000342:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
019974,000343:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
019975,000344:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
019976,000345:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
019977,000346:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
019978,000347: 
019979,000348:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
019980,000349:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
019981,000350:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
019982,000351:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
019983,000352:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
019984,000353:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
019985,000354:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
019986,000355:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
019987,000356:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
019988,000357:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
019989,000358:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
019990,000359:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
019991,000360:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
019992,000361:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
019993,000362:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
019994,000363:                                                                                                  #    NONE
019995,000364:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
019996,000365:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
019997,000366:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

019999,000368:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

020059,000428:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
020060,000429:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020061,000430:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020062,000431:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
020063,000432:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020064,000433: 
020065,000434:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
020066,000435:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
020067,000436:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020068,000437:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
020069,000438:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
020070,000439:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
020071,000440:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
020072,000441:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
020073,000442:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
020074,000443:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
020075,000444:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
020076,000445:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
020077,000446:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
020078,000447:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020079,000448:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
020080,000449:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
020081,000450:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020082,000451:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
020083,000452:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020084,000453:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
020085,000454:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020086,000455:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
020087,000456:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020088,000457:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3

020257,000626:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
020258,000627:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020259,000628:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020260,000629:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
020261,000630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020262,000631: 
020263,000632:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
020264,000633:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
020265,000634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020266,000635:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL

020274,000643:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ

020428,000797:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
020429,000798:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020430,000799:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020431,000800:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
020432,000801:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020433,000802: 
020434,000803:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
020435,000804:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
020436,000805:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
020437,000806:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
020438,000807:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
020439,000808:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
020440,000809:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
020441,000810:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
020442,000811:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020443,000812:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
020444,000813:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
020445,000814:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
020446,000815:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
020447,000816:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
020448,000817:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
020449,000818:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
020450,000819:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020451,000820:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
020452,000821:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
020453,000822:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
020454,000823:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020455,000824:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1

020519,000888:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
020520,000889:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

020524,000893: 
020525,000894:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
020526,000895:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
020527,000896:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
020528,000897:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.

020699,001068:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
020700,001069: 
020701,001070:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020702,001071:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
020703,001072:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
020704,001073:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
020705,001074:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
020706,001075:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
020707,001076:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
020708,001077:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
020709,001078:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
020710,001079:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
020711,001080:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
020712,001081:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
020713,001082:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
020714,001083:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
020715,001084:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
020716,001085:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
020717,001086:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
020718,001087:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
020719,001088:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
020720,001089:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL

Sundance 302 

020790,001159: 
020791,001160:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
020792,001161: 
020793,001162:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020794,001163: 
020795,001164:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
020796,001165:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
020797,001166:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
020798,001167:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
020799,001168:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
020800,001169:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
020801,001170:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
020802,001171:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
020803,001172:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
020804,001173:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
020805,001174:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
020806,001175:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
020807,001176: 
020808,001177:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
020809,001178:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
020810,001179:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
020811,001180: 
020812,001181:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020813,001182:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
020814,001183: 
020815,001184:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
020816,001185: 
020817,001186:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
020818,001187:                                                                                                  #  NONE
020819,001188: 
020820,001189:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
020821,001190: 
020822,001191:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
020823,001192: 
020824,001193: 24,3116                                           BANK     24                                    
020825,001194: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
020826,001195: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
020827,001196: 
020828,001197: 25,2053  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020829,001198: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
020830,001199: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
020831,001200: 25,2054           05271                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
020832,001201: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
020833,001202: 25,2056           45026                           CS       BIT1                                  
020834,001203: 25,2057           71101                           MASK     RADMODES                              
020835,001204: 25,2060           55101                           TS       RADMODES                              
020836,001205: 25,2061           15321                           TCF      TASKOVER                              
020837,001206: 
020838,001207:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
020839,001208: 
020840,001209:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020841,001210:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
020842,001211:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
020843,001212:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
020844,001213:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
020845,001214:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
020846,001215:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
020847,001216:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
020848,001217:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
020849,001218:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
020850,001219:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
020851,001220:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
020852,001221:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
020853,001222:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
020854,001223:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
020855,001224:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
020856,001225: 
020857,001226:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
020858,001227:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020859,001228:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
020860,001229: 
020861,001230:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
020862,001231: 
020863,001232:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
020864,001233:                                                                                                  #  NONE
020865,001234: 
020866,001235:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
020867,001236:

020910,001279:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
020911,001280:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020912,001281:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
020913,001282:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
020914,001283:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
020915,001284:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
020916,001285:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
020917,001286:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
020918,001287:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
020919,001288:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
020920,001289:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
020921,001290:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
020922,001291:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
020923,001292:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
020924,001293:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
020925,001294:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
020926,001295:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
020927,001296:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
020928,001297:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
020929,001298:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
020930,001299:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
020931,001300:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
020932,001301:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
020933,001302:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
020934,001303: 
020935,001304:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
020936,001305:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
020937,001306:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
020938,001307:

020940,001309:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES

020997,001366:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
020998,001367: 
020999,001368:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
021000,001369:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
021001,001370:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
021002,001371:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
021003,001372:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
021004,001373:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
021005,001374:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
021006,001375:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021007,001376:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
021008,001377:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
021009,001378:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
021010,001379:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021011,001380:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
021012,001381:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
021013,001382:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
021014,001383:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
021015,001384:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
021016,001385:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
021017,001386:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
021018,001387:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
021019,001388: 
021020,001389:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021021,001390:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
021022,001391:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
021023,001392:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
021024,001393:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.

021077,001446:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
021078,001447: 
021079,001448:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021080,001449:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
021081,001450:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
021082,001451:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
021083,001452:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
021084,001453:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
021085,001454:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
021086,001455:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
021087,001456:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
021088,001457:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
021089,001458:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
021090,001459:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
021091,001460:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
021092,001461:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
021093,001462:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
021094,001463: 
021095,001464:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
021096,001465:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
021097,001466:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
021098,001467:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
021099,001468:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
021100,001469:

021102,001471:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES

021163,001532: 
021164,001533:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
021165,001534: 
021166,001535:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021167,001536:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
021168,001537:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
021169,001538:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
021170,001539:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
021171,001540:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
021172,001541:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
021173,001542:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
021174,001543:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
021175,001544:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
021176,001545:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
021177,001546:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
021178,001547:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
021179,001548:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.

021265,001634: 25,2351           02001        BIT11+1            OCT      02001                                 
021266,001635: 
021267,001636:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
021268,001637: 
021269,001638:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021270,001639:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
021271,001640:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
021272,001641:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
021273,001642:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
021274,001643:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
021275,001644:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
021276,001645:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
021277,001646:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
021278,001647:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
021279,001648:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
021280,001649:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
021281,001650:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
021282,001651:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
021283,001652:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
021284,001653:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
021285,001654:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
021286,001655:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
021287,001656:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
021288,001657:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
021289,001658:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
021290,001659:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
021291,001660:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
021292,001661: 
021293,001662:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021294,001663:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
021295,001664:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
021296,001665:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021297,001666:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021298,001667: 
021299,001668:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021300,001669:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
021301,001670: 
021302,001671:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021303,001672:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
021304,001673:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
021305,001674: 
021306,001675:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021307,001676:                                                                                                  #     NONE
021308,001677: 
021309,001678:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021310,001679: 
021311,001680:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
021312,001681:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
021313,001682:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
021314,001683: 
021315,001684: 25,2352           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
021316,001685: 25,2353           01116                                    DESRET                                
021317,001686: 25,2354           00271                                    RRNBSW                                
021318,001687: 25,2355           77624                           CALL                                           #  COMPUTES SINES AND COSINES, ORDER Y Z X
021319,001688: 25,2356           47251                                    CDUTRIG                               
021320,001689: 25,2357           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
021321,001690: 25,2360           01105                                    RRTARGET                              
021322,001691: 25,2361           47413                                    *SMNB*

021324,001693: 25,2362           77624                           CALL                                           #  GET RR GIMBAL ANGLES IN PRESENT AND
021325,001694: 25,2363           26105                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.
021326,001695: 25,2364           77776                           EXIT                                           
021327,001696:

021342,001711: 25,2401           75017                           MASK     SURFFBIT                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE
021343,001712: 25,2402           00006                           EXTEND

021345,001714: 25,2404           02444                           TC       NODESSM                               #  NOT ON MOON-CALL FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER
021346,001715: 
021347,001716:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
021348,001717: 
021349,001718:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
021350,001719:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
021351,001720:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021352,001721:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
021353,001722:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
021354,001723:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021355,001724:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
021356,001725:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
021357,001726:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
021358,001727:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
021359,001728:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
021360,001729:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
021361,001730:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
021362,001731:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
021363,001732:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
021364,001733:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
021365,001734:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
021366,001735:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
021367,001736:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
021368,001737:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
021369,001738:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
021370,001739: 
021371,001740:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021372,001741:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.

021513,001882: 25,2546           03512        20.5DEGS           DEC      .11389                                
021514,001883: 
021515,001884:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
021516,001885: 
021517,001886:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021518,001887:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
021519,001888:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
021520,001889:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
021521,001890:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
021522,001891:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
021523,001892:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
021524,001893:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
021525,001894:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
021526,001895:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021527,001896:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
021528,001897:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
021529,001898:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
021530,001899:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
021531,001900:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021532,001901:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
021533,001902:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
021534,001903:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
021535,001904:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
021536,001905:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
021537,001906:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
021538,001907:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
021539,001908:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
021540,001909:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
021541,001910:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
021542,001911:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
021543,001912: 
021544,001913:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021545,001914:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
021546,001915:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
021547,001916:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
021548,001917: 
021549,001918:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021550,001919:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
021551,001920: 
021552,001921:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021553,001922:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
021554,001923: 
021555,001924:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
021556,001925: 
021557,001926:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
021558,001927:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
021559,001928: 
021560,001929:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
021561,001930:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
021562,001931:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
021563,001932: 
021564,001933: 25,2547           41101        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES                              
021565,001934: 
021566,001935: 25,2550           75011                           MASK     REMODBIT

021570,001939: 25,2554           05271        DESLOOP            TC       FIXDELAY                              #  2 SAMPLES PER SECOND.
021571,001940: 25,2555           00062                           DEC      50         B-14                       
021572,001941: 
021573,001942: 25,2556           35014        STDESIG            CAF      BIT11                                 
021574,001943: 25,2557           71101                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  SEE IF GIMBAL LIMIT MONITOR HAS FOUND US
021575,001944: 25,2560           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  OUT OF BOUNDS. IF SO, THIS BIT SHOWS A
021576,001945: 25,2561           12613                           TCF      BADDES                                #  REPOSITION TO BE IN PROGRESS.
021577,001946: 
021578,001947: 25,2562           11101                           CCS      RADMODES                              #  SEE IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE WANTED.

021584,001953: 25,2567           75015                           MASK     BIT10                                 #  PROBLEM (DATA GOOD IF LOCK-ON WANTED OR
021585,001954: 25,2570           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  WITHIN LIMITS IF NOT). IF SO, EXIT AFTER
021586,001955: 25,2571           13502                           TCF      ENDRADAR                              #  CHECKING RR CDU FAIL.
